(****************************************************************

 In this file, we combine the facts from `precomp_ess_surj.v`
 and `precomp_fully_faithful.v`. We show that if we have a fully
 faithful and essential surjective functor `F : C₁ ⟶ C₂` and a
 univalent category `D`, then we have an adjoint equivalence
 between `[ C₂ , D ]` and `[ C₁ , D ]` (the functor is given
 by precomposition). We also give some functions to use this
 adjoint equivalence.

 ****************************************************************)

  Defined.

  Let L : [ C₂ , D ] ⟶ [ C₁ , D ]
    := pre_composition_functor C₁ C₂ (pr1 D) F.
  Let R : [ C₁ , D ] ⟶ [ C₂ , D ]
    := right_adjoint precomp_adjoint_equivalence.
  Let ε : nat_z_iso (R ∙ L) (functor_identity _)
    := counit_nat_z_iso_from_adj_equivalence_of_cats
         precomp_adjoint_equivalence.
  Let η : nat_z_iso (functor_identity _) (L ∙ R)
    := unit_nat_z_iso_from_adj_equivalence_of_cats
         precomp_adjoint_equivalence.

  Definition lift_functor_along
             (G : C₁ ⟶ D)
    : C₂ ⟶ D
    := R G.

  Definition lift_functor_along_comm
             (G : C₁ ⟶ D)
    : nat_z_iso (F ∙ lift_functor_along G) G
    := nat_z_iso_from_z_iso _ (nat_z_iso_pointwise_z_iso ε G).

η:= unit_nat_z_iso_from_adj_equivalence_of_cats

  [C₂, pr1 D] [C₁, pr1 D]

  (pre_composition_functor C₁ C₂ 
     (pr1 D) F)

End PrecompEquivalence.

Section WeakEquivalenceProperties.

  Context {C1 C2 D1 D2 : category}
          (F : functor C1 C2) (G : functor D1 D2).

  
C1, C2, D1, D2: category
F: C1 ⟶ C2
G: D1 ⟶ D2
F_ff: fully_faithful F
G_ff: fully_faithful G
fully_faithful (pair_functor F G)

  
C1, C2, D1, D2: category
F: C1 ⟶ C2
G: D1 ⟶ D2
F_ff: fully_faithful F
G_ff: fully_faithful G
fully_faithful (pair_functor F G)


    
C1, C2, D1, D2: category
F: C1 ⟶ C2
G: D1 ⟶ D2
F_ff: fully_faithful F
G_ff: fully_faithful G
cd, cd': category_binproduct C1 D1
cd2: category_binproduct C2 D2 ⟦ 
pair_functor F G cd, pair_functor F G cd' ⟧
iscontr (hfiber # (pair_functor F G) cd2)


    
C1, C2, D1, D2: category
F: C1 ⟶ C2
G: D1 ⟶ D2
F_ff: fully_faithful F
G_ff: fully_faithful G
cd, cd': category_binproduct C1 D1
cd2: category_binproduct C2 D2 ⟦ 
pair_functor F G cd, pair_functor F G cd' ⟧
hfiber # (pair_functor F G) cd2
≃ hfiber # F (pr1 cd2) × hfiber # G (pr2 cd2)
C1, C2, D1, D2: category
F: C1 ⟶ C2
G: D1 ⟶ D2
F_ff: fully_faithful F
G_ff: fully_faithful G
cd, cd': category_binproduct C1 D1
cd2: category_binproduct C2 D2 ⟦ 
pair_functor F G cd, pair_functor F G cd' ⟧
hfiberprod: hfiber # (pair_functor F G) cd2
≃ hfiber # F (pr1 cd2)
  × hfiber # G (pr2 cd2)
iscontr (hfiber # (pair_functor F G) cd2)

    
C1, C2, D1, D2: category
F: C1 ⟶ C2
G: D1 ⟶ D2
F_ff: fully_faithful F
G_ff: fully_faithful G
cd, cd': category_binproduct C1 D1
cd2: category_binproduct C2 D2 ⟦ 
pair_functor F G cd, pair_functor F G cd' ⟧
hfiber # (pair_functor F G) cd2
≃ hfiber # F (pr1 cd2) × hfiber # G (pr2 cd2)

cd2: category_binproduct C2 D2 ⟦ 
pair_functor F G cd, pair_functor F G cd' ⟧
∏ x : hfiber # (pair_functor F G) cd2, ?g (?f x) = x
C1, C2, D1, D2: category
F: C1 ⟶ C2
G: D1 ⟶ D2
F_ff: fully_faithful F
G_ff: fully_faithful G
cd, cd': category_binproduct C1 D1
cd2: category_binproduct C2 D2 ⟦ 
pair_functor F G cd, pair_functor F G cd' ⟧
∏ y : hfiber # F (pr1 cd2) × hfiber # G (pr2 cd2),
?f (?g y) = y

      
C1, C2, D1, D2: category
F: C1 ⟶ C2
G: D1 ⟶ D2
F_ff: fully_faithful F
G_ff: fully_faithful G
cd, cd': category_binproduct C1 D1
cd2: category_binproduct C2 D2 ⟦ 
pair_functor F G cd, pair_functor F G cd' ⟧
hfiber # (pair_functor F G) cd2
→ hfiber # F (pr1 cd2) × hfiber # G (pr2 cd2)

C1, C2, D1, D2: category
F: C1 ⟶ C2
G: D1 ⟶ D2
F_ff: fully_faithful F
G_ff: fully_faithful G
cd, cd': category_binproduct C1 D1
cd2: category_binproduct C2 D2 ⟦ 
pair_functor F G cd, pair_functor F G cd' ⟧
xy: hfiber # F (pr1 cd2) × hfiber # G (pr2 cd2)
transportf
  (λ _ : C2 ⟦ pr1 (pair_functor F G cd),
         pr1 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧,
   D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
   pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧) (pr21 xy)
  (pr2
     (# (pair_functor F G)
        (catbinprodmor (pr11 xy) (pr12 xy)))) = ?b

            exact (toforallpaths _ _ _ (transportf_const (pr21 xy) ( D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd), pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧)) (pr2 (# (pair_functor F G) (catbinprodmor (pr11 xy) (pr12 xy))))).
          
C1, C2, D1, D2: category
F: C1 ⟶ C2
G: D1 ⟶ D2
F_ff: fully_faithful F
G_ff: fully_faithful G
cd, cd': category_binproduct C1 D1
cd2: category_binproduct C2 D2 ⟦ 
pair_functor F G cd, pair_functor F G cd' ⟧
xy: hfiber # F (pr1 cd2) × hfiber # G (pr2 cd2)
idfun
  (D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
   pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧)
  (pr2
     (# (pair_functor F G)
        (catbinprodmor (pr11 xy) (pr12 xy)))) =
pr2 cd2

          exact (pr22 xy).
      
C1, C2, D1, D2: category
F: C1 ⟶ C2
G: D1 ⟶ D2
F_ff: fully_faithful F
G_ff: fully_faithful G
cd, cd': category_binproduct C1 D1
cd2: category_binproduct C2 D2 ⟦ 
pair_functor F G cd, pair_functor F G cd' ⟧
∏ x : hfiber # (pair_functor F G) cd2,
(λ xy : hfiber # F (pr1 cd2) × hfiber # G (pr2 cd2),
 catbinprodmor (pr11 xy) (pr12 xy),,
 total2_paths_f (pr21 xy)
   (toforallpaths
      (λ _ : (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd), F (pr1 cd') ⟧,
              D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
              pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧)
               (# F (pr11 xy)),
       (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd), F (pr1 cd') ⟧,
        D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
        pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧) (pr1 cd2))
      (transportf
         (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd), F (pr1 cd') ⟧,
          D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
          pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧) (pr21 xy))
      (idfun
         (D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
          pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧))
      (transportf_const (pr21 xy)
         (D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
          pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧))
      (pr2
         (# (pair_functor F G)
            (catbinprodmor (pr11 xy) (pr12 xy)))) @
    pr22 xy))
  ((λ x0 : hfiber # (pair_functor F G) cd2,
    (pr11 x0,, maponpaths pr1 (pr2 x0)),,
    pr21 x0,,
    idpath (pr2 (# (pair_functor F G) (pr1 x0))) @
    maponpaths pr2 (let X := pr2 x0 in X)) x) = x
 
C1, C2, D1, D2: category
F: C1 ⟶ C2
G: D1 ⟶ D2
F_ff: fully_faithful F
G_ff: fully_faithful G
cd, cd': category_binproduct C1 D1
cd2: category_binproduct C2 D2 ⟦ 
pair_functor F G cd, pair_functor F G cd' ⟧
x: hfiber # (pair_functor F G) cd2
(λ xy : hfiber # F (pr1 cd2) × hfiber # G (pr2 cd2),
 catbinprodmor (pr11 xy) (pr12 xy),,
 total2_paths_f (pr21 xy)
   (toforallpaths
      (λ _ : (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd), F (pr1 cd') ⟧,
              D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
              pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧)
               (# F (pr11 xy)),
       (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd), F (pr1 cd') ⟧,
        D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
        pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧) (pr1 cd2))
      (transportf
         (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd), F (pr1 cd') ⟧,
          D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
          pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧) (pr21 xy))
      (idfun
         (D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
          pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧))
      (transportf_const (pr21 xy)
         (D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
          pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧))
      (pr2
         (# (pair_functor F G)
            (catbinprodmor (pr11 xy) (pr12 xy)))) @
    pr22 xy))
  ((λ x : hfiber # (pair_functor F G) cd2,
    (pr11 x,, maponpaths pr1 (pr2 x)),,
    pr21 x,,
    idpath (pr2 (# (pair_functor F G) (pr1 x))) @
    maponpaths pr2 (let X := pr2 x in X)) x) = x

        
C1, C2, D1, D2: category
F: C1 ⟶ C2
G: D1 ⟶ D2
F_ff: fully_faithful F
G_ff: fully_faithful G
cd, cd': category_binproduct C1 D1
cd2: category_binproduct C2 D2 ⟦ 
pair_functor F G cd, pair_functor F G cd' ⟧
x: hfiber # (pair_functor F G) cd2
pr1
  (catbinprodmor
     (pr11 ((λ x : hfiber # (pair_functor F G) cd2,
             (pr11 x,, maponpaths pr1 (pr2 x)),,
             pr21 x,,
             idpath
               (pr2 (# (pair_functor F G) (pr1 x))) @
             maponpaths pr2 (let X := pr2 x in X)) x))
     (pr12 ((λ x : hfiber # (pair_functor F G) cd2,
             (pr11 x,, maponpaths pr1 (pr2 x)),,
             pr21 x,,
             idpath
               (pr2 (# (pair_functor F G) (pr1 x))) @
             maponpaths pr2 (let X := pr2 x in X)) x)),,
   total2_paths_f
     (pr21 ((λ x : hfiber # (pair_functor F G) cd2,
             (pr11 x,, maponpaths pr1 (pr2 x)),,
             pr21 x,,
             idpath
               (pr2 (# (pair_functor F G) (pr1 x))) @
             maponpaths pr2 (let X := pr2 x in X)) x))
     (toforallpaths
        (λ _ : (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd), F (pr1 cd') ⟧,
                D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧)
                 (# F
                    (pr11 ((λ x : hfiber
                                    # (pair_functor F
                                         G) cd2,
                            (pr11 x,,
                             maponpaths pr1 (pr2 x)),,
                            pr21 x,,
                            idpath (pr2 (# ... ...)) @
                            maponpaths pr2
                              (let X := pr2 x in X)) x))),
         (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd), F (pr1 cd') ⟧,
          D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
          pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧) (pr1 cd2))
        (transportf
           (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd), F (pr1 cd') ⟧,
            D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
            pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧)
           (pr21 ((λ x : hfiber # (pair_functor F G)
                           cd2,
                   (pr11 x,, maponpaths pr1 (pr2 x)),,
                   pr21 x,,
                   idpath
                     (pr2
                        (# (pair_functor F G) (pr1 x))) @
                   maponpaths pr2
                     (let X := pr2 x in X)) x)))
        (idfun
           (D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
            pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧))
        (transportf_const
           (pr21 ((λ x : hfiber # (pair_functor F G)
                           cd2,
                   (pr11 x,, maponpaths pr1 (pr2 x)),,
                   pr21 x,,
                   idpath
                     (pr2
                        (# (pair_functor F G) (pr1 x))) @
                   maponpaths pr2
                     (let X := pr2 x in X)) x))
           (D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
            pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧))
        (pr2
           (# (pair_functor F G)
              (catbinprodmor
                 (pr11 ((λ x : hfiber
                                 # (pair_functor F G)
                                 cd2,
                         (pr11 x,,
                          maponpaths pr1 (pr2 x)),,
                         pr21 x,,
                         idpath (pr2 (# ... ...)) @
                         maponpaths pr2
                           (let X := pr2 x in X)) x))
                 (pr12 ((λ x : hfiber
                                 # (pair_functor F G)
                                 cd2,
                         (pr11 x,,
                          maponpaths pr1 (pr2 x)),,
                         pr21 x,,
                         idpath (pr2 (# ... ...)) @
                         maponpaths pr2
                           (let X := pr2 x in X)) x))))) @
      pr22 ((λ x : hfiber # (pair_functor F G) cd2,
             (pr11 x,, maponpaths pr1 (pr2 x)),,
             pr21 x,,
             idpath
               (pr2 (# (pair_functor F G) (pr1 x))) @
             maponpaths pr2 (let X := pr2 x in X)) x))) =
pr1 x
C1, C2, D1, D2: category
F: C1 ⟶ C2
G: D1 ⟶ D2
F_ff: fully_faithful F
G_ff: fully_faithful G
cd, cd': category_binproduct C1 D1
cd2: category_binproduct C2 D2 ⟦ 
pair_functor F G cd, pair_functor F G cd' ⟧
x: hfiber # (pair_functor F G) cd2
transportf
  (λ x : category_binproduct C1 D1 ⟦ cd, cd' ⟧,
   # (pair_functor F G) x = cd2) 
  ?p
  (pr2
     (catbinprodmor
        (pr11 ((λ x : hfiber # (pair_functor F G) cd2,
                (pr11 x,, maponpaths pr1 (pr2 x)),,
                pr21 x,,
                idpath
                  (pr2 (# (pair_functor F G) (pr1 x))) @
                maponpaths pr2 (let X := pr2 x in X))
                 x))
        (pr12 ((λ x : hfiber # (pair_functor F G) cd2,
                (pr11 x,, maponpaths pr1 (pr2 x)),,
                pr21 x,,
                idpath
                  (pr2 (# (pair_functor F G) (pr1 x))) @
                maponpaths pr2 (let X := pr2 x in X))
                 x)),,
      total2_paths_f
        (pr21 ((λ x : hfiber # (pair_functor F G) cd2,
                (pr11 x,, maponpaths pr1 (pr2 x)),,
                pr21 x,,
                idpath
                  (pr2 (# (pair_functor F G) (pr1 x))) @
                maponpaths pr2 (let X := pr2 x in X))
                 x))
        (toforallpaths
           (λ _ : (λ _ : 
                      C2 ⟦ 
                      F (pr1 cd), 
                      F (pr1 cd') ⟧,
                   D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                   pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧)
                    (# F
                       (pr11 
                        ((λ 
                        x : 
                        hfiber # 
                        (pair_functor F G) cd2,
                        (pr11 x,,
                        maponpaths pr1 (pr2 x)),,
                        pr21 x,,
                        idpath (pr2 ...) @
                        maponpaths pr2 (... X)) x))),
            (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd), F (pr1 cd') ⟧,
             D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
             pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧) 
              (pr1 cd2))
           (transportf
              (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd), F (pr1 cd') ⟧,
               D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
               pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧)
              (pr21 ((λ x : 
                        hfiber # 
                        (pair_functor F G) cd2,
                      (pr11 x,, maponpaths pr1 (pr2 x)),,
                      pr21 x,,
                      idpath
                        (pr2
                        (# (pair_functor F G) (pr1 x))) @
                      maponpaths pr2
                        (let X := pr2 x in X)) x)))
           (idfun
              (D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
               pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧))
           (transportf_const
              (pr21 ((λ x : 
                        hfiber # 
                        (pair_functor F G) cd2,
                      (pr11 x,, maponpaths pr1 (pr2 x)),,
                      pr21 x,,
                      idpath
                        (pr2
                        (# (pair_functor F G) (pr1 x))) @
                      maponpaths pr2
                        (let X := pr2 x in X)) x))
              (D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
               pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧))
           (pr2
              (# (pair_functor F G)
                 (catbinprodmor
                    (pr11 
                     ((λ 
                       x : 
                        hfiber # 
                        (pair_functor F G) cd2,
                       (pr11 x,,
                        maponpaths pr1 (pr2 x)),,
                       pr21 x,,
                       idpath (pr2 ...) @
                       maponpaths pr2 (... X)) x))
                    (pr12 
                     ((λ 
                       x : 
                        hfiber # 
                        (pair_functor F G) cd2,
                       (pr11 x,,
                        maponpaths pr1 (pr2 x)),,
                       pr21 x,,
                       idpath (pr2 ...) @
                       maponpaths pr2 (... X)) x))))) @
         pr22 ((λ x : hfiber # (pair_functor F G) cd2,
                (pr11 x,, maponpaths pr1 (pr2 x)),,
                pr21 x,,
                idpath
                  (pr2 (# (pair_functor F G) (pr1 x))) @
                maponpaths pr2 (let X := pr2 x in X))
                 x)))) = 
pr2 x

        
C1, C2, D1, D2: category
F: C1 ⟶ C2

G_ff: fully_faithful G

cd2: category_binproduct C2 D2 ⟦ 
pair_functor F G cd, pair_functor F G cd' ⟧
x: hfiber # (pair_functor F G) cd2
pr1
  (catbinprodmor
     (pr11 ((λ x : hfiber # (pair_functor F G) cd2,
             (pr11 x,, maponpaths pr1 (pr2 x)),,
             pr21 x,,
             idpath
               (pr2 (# (pair_functor F G) (pr1 x))) @
             maponpaths pr2 (let X := pr2 x in X)) x))
     (pr12 ((λ x : hfiber # (pair_functor F G) cd2,
             (pr11 x,, maponpaths pr1 (pr2 x)),,
             pr21 x,,

               (pr2 (# (pair_functor F G) (pr1 x))) @
             maponpaths pr2 (let X := pr2 x in X)) x)),,
   total2_paths_f
     (pr21 ((λ x : hfiber # (pair_functor F G) cd2,
             (pr11 x,, maponpaths pr1 (pr2 x)),,
             pr21 x,,
             idpath
               (pr2 (# (pair_functor F G) (pr1 x))) @
             maponpaths pr2 (let X := pr2 x in X)) x))
     (toforallpaths
        (λ _ : (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd), F (pr1 cd') ⟧,
                D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧)

                    (pr11 ((λ x : hfiber
                                    # (pair_functor F
                                         G) cd2,
                            (pr11 x,,
                             maponpaths pr1 (pr2 x)),,
                            pr21 x,,

          D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
          pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧) (pr1 cd2))
        (transportf
           (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd), F (pr1 cd') ⟧,
            D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
            pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧)

                           cd2,

                   pr21 x,,

                     (pr2

                   maponpaths pr2
                     (let X := pr2 x in X)) x)))

           (D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
            pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧))
        (transportf_const
           (pr21 ((λ x : hfiber # (pair_functor F G)
                           cd2,
                   (pr11 x,, maponpaths pr1 (pr2 x)),,
                   pr21 x,,

                   maponpaths pr2
                     (let X := pr2 x in X)) x))
           (D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
            pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧))
        (pr2

                 (pr11 ((λ x : hfiber
                                 # (pair_functor F G)

             pr21 x,,
             idpath
               (pr2 (# (pair_functor F G) (pr1 x))) @

pr1 x

C1, C2, D1, D2: category
F: C1 ⟶ C2
G: D1 ⟶ D2
F_ff: fully_faithful F
G_ff: fully_faithful G
cd, cd': category_binproduct C1 D1
cd2: category_binproduct C2 D2 ⟦ 
pair_functor F G cd, pair_functor F G cd' ⟧
x: hfiber # (pair_functor F G) cd2
transportf
  (λ x : category_binproduct C1 D1 ⟦ cd, cd' ⟧,
   # (pair_functor F G) x = cd2) (idpath (pr1 x))
  (pr2
     (catbinprodmor
        (pr11 ((λ x : hfiber # (pair_functor F G) cd2,
                (pr11 x,, maponpaths pr1 (pr2 x)),,
                pr21 x,,
                idpath
                  (pr2 (# (pair_functor F G) (pr1 x))) @
                maponpaths pr2 (let X := pr2 x in X))
                 x))
        (pr12 ((λ x : hfiber # (pair_functor F G) cd2,
                (pr11 x,, maponpaths pr1 (pr2 x)),,
                pr21 x,,
                idpath
                  (pr2 (# (pair_functor F G) (pr1 x))) @
                maponpaths pr2 (let X := pr2 x in X))
                 x)),,
      total2_paths_f
        (pr21 ((λ x : hfiber # (pair_functor F G) cd2,
                (pr11 x,, maponpaths pr1 (pr2 x)),,
                pr21 x,,
                idpath
                  (pr2 (# (pair_functor F G) (pr1 x))) @
                maponpaths pr2 (let X := pr2 x in X))
                 x))
        (toforallpaths
           (λ _ : (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd), F (pr1 cd')
                         ⟧,
                   D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                   pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧)
                    (# F
                       (pr11 ((λ x : hfiber
                                       # (pair_functor
                                            F G) cd2,
                               (pr11 x,,
                                maponpaths pr1 (pr2 x)),,
                               pr21 x,,
                               idpath (pr2 ...) @
                               maponpaths pr2 (... X))
                                x))),
            (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd), F (pr1 cd') ⟧,
             D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
             pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧) (pr1 cd2))
           (transportf
              (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd), F (pr1 cd') ⟧,
               D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
               pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧)
              (pr21 ((λ x : hfiber
                              # (pair_functor F G) cd2,
                      (pr11 x,, maponpaths pr1 (pr2 x)),,
                      pr21 x,,
                      idpath
                        (pr2
                           (# (pair_functor F G)
                              (pr1 x))) @
                      maponpaths pr2
                        (let X := pr2 x in X)) x)))
           (idfun
              (D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
               pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧))
           (transportf_const
              (pr21 ((λ x : hfiber
                              # (pair_functor F G) cd2,
                      (pr11 x,, maponpaths pr1 (pr2 x)),,
                      pr21 x,,
                      idpath
                        (pr2
                           (# (pair_functor F G)
                              (pr1 x))) @
                      maponpaths pr2
                        (let X := pr2 x in X)) x))
              (D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
               pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧))
           (pr2
              (# (pair_functor F G)
                 (catbinprodmor
                    (pr11 ((λ x : hfiber
                                    # (pair_functor F
                                         G) cd2,
                            (pr11 x,,
                             maponpaths pr1 (pr2 x)),,
                            pr21 x,,
                            idpath (pr2 ...) @

                                         G) cd2,

                            pr21 x,,

                (pr11 x,, maponpaths pr1 (pr2 x)),,
                pr21 x,,
                idpath
                  (pr2 (# (pair_functor F G) (pr1 x))) @
                maponpaths pr2 (let X := pr2 x in X))

C1, C2, D1, D2: category
F: C1 ⟶ C2
G: D1 ⟶ D2
F_ff: fully_faithful F
G_ff: fully_faithful G
cd, cd': category_binproduct C1 D1
cd2: category_binproduct C2 D2 ⟦ 
pair_functor F G cd, pair_functor F G cd' ⟧
∏ y : hfiber # F (pr1 cd2) × hfiber # G (pr2 cd2),
(λ x : hfiber # (pair_functor F G) cd2,
 (pr11 x,, maponpaths pr1 (pr2 x)),,
 pr21 x,,
 idpath (pr2 (# (pair_functor F G) (pr1 x))) @
 maponpaths pr2 (let X := pr2 x in X))
  ((λ xy : hfiber # F (pr1 cd2) × hfiber # G (pr2 cd2),
    catbinprodmor (pr11 xy) (pr12 xy),,
    total2_paths_f (pr21 xy)
      (toforallpaths
         (λ _ : (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd), F (pr1 cd') ⟧,
                 D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                 pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧)
                  (# F (pr11 xy)),
          (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd), F (pr1 cd') ⟧,
           D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
           pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧) (pr1 cd2))
         (transportf
            (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd), F (pr1 cd') ⟧,
             D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
             pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧) (pr21 xy))
         (idfun
            (D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
             pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧))
         (transportf_const (pr21 xy)
            (D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
             pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧))
         (pr2
            (# (pair_functor F G)
               (catbinprodmor (pr11 xy) (pr12 xy)))) @
       pr22 xy)) y) = y

C1, C2, D1, D2: category
F: C1 ⟶ C2

                  × hfiber # G (pr2 cd2),
           catbinprodmor (pr11 xy) (pr12 xy),,
           total2_paths_f (pr21 xy)

                        ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),

                  pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧)
                   (pr1 cd2))
                (transportf
                   (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd), F (pr1 cd')
                          ⟧,
                    D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                    pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧)

                   (D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                    pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧))

                      (catbinprodmor (pr11 xy)
                         (pr12 xy)))) @ pr22 xy)) y),,

      (pr2
         ((λ xy : hfiber # F (pr1 cd2)
                  × hfiber # G (pr2 cd2),
           catbinprodmor (pr11 xy) (pr12 xy),,
           total2_paths_f (pr21 xy)
             (toforallpaths
                (λ _ : (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F ..., F ... ⟧,
                        D2 ⟦ pr2 (...), pr2 (...) ⟧)
                         (# F (pr11 xy)),
                 (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (...), F (...) ⟧,
                  D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                  pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧)
                   (pr1 cd2))
                (transportf
                   (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd), F (pr1 cd')
                          ⟧,
                    D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                    pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧)
                   (pr21 xy))
                (idfun
                   (D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                    pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧))
                (transportf_const (pr21 xy)
                   (D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                    pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧))
                (pr2
                   (# (pair_functor F G)
                      (catbinprodmor (pr11 xy)
                         (pr12 xy)))) @ pr22 xy)) y))),,
   pr21 ((λ xy : hfiber # F (pr1 cd2)
                 × hfiber # G (pr2 cd2),
          catbinprodmor (pr11 xy) (pr12 xy),,
          total2_paths_f (pr21 xy)
            (toforallpaths
               (λ _ : (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd),
                             F (pr1 cd') ⟧,
                       D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                       pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧)
                        (# F (pr11 xy)),

                 D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                 pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧)
                  (pr1 cd2))
               (transportf
                  (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd), F (pr1 cd')
                         ⟧,
                   D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                   pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧)

                   pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧))
               (pr2
                  (# (pair_functor F G)
                     (catbinprodmor (pr11 xy)
                        (pr12 xy)))) @ pr22 xy)) y),,
   idpath
     (pr2
        (# (pair_functor F G)
           (pr1
              ((λ xy : hfiber # F (pr1 cd2)
                       × hfiber # G (pr2 cd2),
                catbinprodmor (pr11 xy) (pr12 xy),,

                  (toforallpaths
                     (λ _ : (...) (...),
                      (λ ..., ...) (pr1 cd2))
                     (transportf
                        (λ _ : ..., D2 ⟦ ..., ... ⟧)
                        (pr21 xy))

                     (transportf_const (pr21 xy)

                 y)))) @
   maponpaths pr2
     (let X :=
        pr2
          ((λ xy : hfiber # F (pr1 cd2)

C1, C2, D1, D2: category
F: C1 ⟶ C2
G: D1 ⟶ D2
F_ff: fully_faithful F
G_ff: fully_faithful G
cd, cd': category_binproduct C1 D1
cd2: category_binproduct C2 D2 ⟦ 
pair_functor F G cd, pair_functor F G cd' ⟧
y: hfiber # F (pr1 cd2) × hfiber # G (pr2 cd2)
transportf
  (λ _ : hfiber # F (pr1 cd2), hfiber # G (pr2 cd2))
  ?p
  (pr2
     ((pr11 ((λ xy : hfiber # F (pr1 cd2)
                     × hfiber # G (pr2 cd2),
              catbinprodmor (pr11 xy) (pr12 xy),,
              total2_paths_f

                   (λ _ :

                        F (pr1 cd') ⟧,
                     D2 ⟦

                     pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧)

                       pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧)
                      (pr21 xy))

                      (D2 ⟦ 
                       pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                       pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧))
                   (transportf_const 
                      (pr21 xy)
                      (D2 ⟦ 
                       pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                       pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧))
                   (pr2
                      (# (pair_functor F G)
                        (catbinprodmor 
                        (pr11 xy) 
                        (pr12 xy)))) @ pr22 xy)) y),,
       maponpaths pr1
         (pr2
            ((λ xy : hfiber # F (pr1 cd2)
                     × hfiber # G (pr2 cd2),
              catbinprodmor (pr11 xy) (pr12 xy),,
              total2_paths_f 
                (pr21 xy)

                   (λ _ : 
                       (λ _ : ..., D2 ⟦ ..., ... ⟧)
                        (# F (pr11 xy)),

                     D2 ⟦ pr2 ..., pr2 ... ⟧)
                      (pr1 cd2))
                   (transportf
                      (λ 
                       _ : C2 ⟦ F ..., F ... ⟧,
                       D2 ⟦ pr2 (...), pr2 (...) ⟧)
                      (pr21 xy))
                   (idfun
                      (D2 ⟦ 
                       pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                       pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧))
                   (transportf_const 
                      (pr21 xy)

                       pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                       pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧))
                   (pr2
                      (# (pair_functor F G)
                        (catbinprodmor 
                        (pr11 xy) 
                        (pr12 xy)))) @ pr22 xy)) y))),,
      pr21 ((λ xy : hfiber # F (pr1 cd2)
                    × hfiber # G (pr2 cd2),
             catbinprodmor (pr11 xy) (pr12 xy),,
             total2_paths_f 
               (pr21 xy)
               (toforallpaths
                  (λ _ :

                      pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧)
                     (pr21 xy))
                  (idfun
                     (D2 ⟦ 
                      pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                      pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧))
                  (transportf_const 
                     (pr21 xy)
                     (D2 ⟦ 
                      pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                      pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧))
                  (pr2
                     (# (pair_functor F G)
                        (catbinprodmor 
                        (pr11 xy) 
                        (pr12 xy)))) @ pr22 xy)) y),,
      idpath
        (pr2
           (# (pair_functor F G)
              (pr1
                 ((λ xy : 
                      hfiber # F (pr1 cd2)
                      × hfiber # G (pr2 cd2),
                   catbinprodmor (pr11 xy) (pr12 xy),,
                   total2_paths_f 
                     (pr21 xy)
                     (toforallpaths
                        (λ _ : ..., ... ...)
                        (transportf (...) (pr21 xy))
                        (idfun (...))
                        (transportf_const 
                        (pr21 xy) 
                        (...)) 
                        (pr2 (...)) @ pr22 xy)) y)))) @
      maponpaths pr2
        (let X :=
           pr2
             ((λ xy : hfiber # F (pr1 cd2)
                      × hfiber # G (pr2 cd2),
               catbinprodmor (pr11 xy) (pr12 xy),,
               total2_paths_f 
                 (pr21 xy)
                 (toforallpaths
                    (λ _ : (...) (...),
                     (λ ..., ...) (pr1 cd2))
                    (transportf
                       (λ _ : ..., D2 ⟦ ..., ... ⟧)
                       (pr21 xy))
                    (idfun (D2 ⟦ pr2 ..., pr2 ... ⟧))
                    (transportf_const 
                       (pr21 xy)
                       (D2 ⟦ pr2 ..., pr2 ... ⟧))
                    (pr2 (# (...) (...))) @ pr22 xy))
                y) in
         X))) = pr2 y

        
C1, C2, D1, D2: category
F: C1 ⟶ C2
G: D1 ⟶ D2
F_ff: fully_faithful F
G_ff: fully_faithful G
cd, cd': category_binproduct C1 D1
cd2: category_binproduct C2 D2 ⟦ 
pair_functor F G cd, pair_functor F G cd' ⟧
y: hfiber # F (pr1 cd2) × hfiber # G (pr2 cd2)
pr1
  ((pr11 ((λ xy : hfiber # F (pr1 cd2)
                  × hfiber # G (pr2 cd2),
           catbinprodmor (pr11 xy) (pr12 xy),,
           total2_paths_f (pr21 xy)
             (toforallpaths
                (λ _ : (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd),
                              F (pr1 cd') ⟧,
                        D2
                        ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                        pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧)
                         (# F (pr11 xy)),
                 (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd), F (pr1 cd') ⟧,
                  D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                  pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧)
                   (pr1 cd2))
                (transportf
                   (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd), F (pr1 cd')
                          ⟧,
                    D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                    pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧)
                   (pr21 xy))
                (idfun
                   (D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                    pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧))
                (transportf_const (pr21 xy)
                   (D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                    pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧))
                (pr2
                   (# (pair_functor F G)
                      (catbinprodmor (pr11 xy)
                         (pr12 xy)))) @ pr22 xy)) y),,
    maponpaths pr1
      (pr2
         ((λ xy : hfiber # F (pr1 cd2)
                  × hfiber # G (pr2 cd2),
           catbinprodmor (pr11 xy) (pr12 xy),,
           total2_paths_f (pr21 xy)
             (toforallpaths
                (λ _ : (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F ..., F ... ⟧,
                        D2 ⟦ pr2 (...), pr2 (...) ⟧)
                         (# F (pr11 xy)),

                   (pr1 cd2))
                (transportf
                   (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd), F (pr1 cd')
                          ⟧,
                    D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                    pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧)
                   (pr21 xy))
                (idfun
                   (D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                    pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧))
                (transportf_const (pr21 xy)
                   (D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                    pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧))
                (pr2
                   (# (pair_functor F G)
                      (catbinprodmor (pr11 xy)
                         (pr12 xy)))) @ pr22 xy)) y))),,
   pr21 ((λ xy : hfiber # F (pr1 cd2)
                 × hfiber # G (pr2 cd2),
          catbinprodmor (pr11 xy) (pr12 xy),,
          total2_paths_f (pr21 xy)
            (toforallpaths
               (λ _ : (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd),
                             F (pr1 cd') ⟧,
                       D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                       pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧)
                        (# F (pr11 xy)),
                (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd), F (pr1 cd') ⟧,
                 D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                 pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧)
                  (pr1 cd2))
               (transportf
                  (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd), F (pr1 cd')
                         ⟧,
                   D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                   pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧)
                  (pr21 xy))
               (idfun
                  (D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                   pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧))
               (transportf_const (pr21 xy)
                  (D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                   pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧))
               (pr2
                  (# (pair_functor F G)
                     (catbinprodmor (pr11 xy)
                        (pr12 xy)))) @ pr22 xy)) y),,
   idpath
     (pr2
        (# (pair_functor F G)
           (pr1
              ((λ xy : hfiber # F (pr1 cd2)
                       × hfiber # G (pr2 cd2),
                catbinprodmor (pr11 xy) (pr12 xy),,
                total2_paths_f (pr21 xy)
                  (toforallpaths
                     (λ _ : (...) (...),
                      (λ ..., ...) (pr1 cd2))
                     (transportf
                        (λ _ : ..., D2 ⟦ ..., ... ⟧)
                        (pr21 xy))
                     (idfun (D2 ⟦ pr2 ..., pr2 ... ⟧))
                     (transportf_const (pr21 xy)
                        (D2 ⟦ pr2 ..., pr2 ... ⟧))
                     (pr2 (# (...) (...))) @ pr22 xy))
                 y)))) @
   maponpaths pr2
     (let X :=
        pr2
          ((λ xy : hfiber # F (pr1 cd2)

                 (pr2
                    (# (pair_functor F G)
                       (catbinprodmor (pr11 xy)
                          (pr12 xy)))) @ pr22 xy)) y)
        in
      X)) = pr1 y

F: C1 ⟶ C2
G: D1 ⟶ D2
F_ff: fully_faithful F
G_ff: fully_faithful G
cd, cd': category_binproduct C1 D1
cd2: category_binproduct C2 D2 ⟦ 
pair_functor F G cd, pair_functor F G cd' ⟧
y: hfiber # F (pr1 cd2) × hfiber # G (pr2 cd2)
transportf
  (λ x : C1 ⟦ pr1 cd, pr1 cd' ⟧, # F x = pr1 cd2) 
  ?p
  (pr21 ((pr11 ((λ xy : hfiber # F (pr1 cd2)
                        × 
                        hfiber # G (pr2 cd2),
                 catbinprodmor (pr11 xy) (pr12 xy),,
                 total2_paths_f 
                   (pr21 xy)
                   (toforallpaths
                      (λ

                        (λ

                        pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧)

                        ⟦

                        pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧)
                        (pr21 xy))

                    (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd),
                           F (pr1 cd') ⟧,
                     D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                     pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧)
                      (pr1 cd2))
                   (transportf
                      (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd),
                             F (pr1 cd') ⟧,
                       D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                       pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧)
                      (pr21 xy))
                   (idfun
                      (D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                       pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧))
                   (transportf_const (pr21 xy)
                      (D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                       pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧))
                   (pr2
                      (# (pair_functor F G)
                         (catbinprodmor (pr11 xy)
                            (pr12 xy)))) @ pr22 xy)) y))),,
      pr21 ((λ xy : hfiber # F (pr1 cd2)
                    × hfiber # G (pr2 cd2),
             catbinprodmor (pr11 xy) (pr12 xy),,
             total2_paths_f (pr21 xy)
               (toforallpaths
                  (λ _ : (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd),
                                F (pr1 cd') ⟧,
                          D2
                          ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                          pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧)
                           (# F (pr11 xy)),
                   (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd), F (pr1 cd')
                          ⟧,
                    D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                    pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧)
                     (pr1 cd2))
                  (transportf
                     (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd),
                            F (pr1 cd') ⟧,
                      D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                      pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧)
                     (pr21 xy))
                  (idfun
                     (D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                      pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧))
                  (transportf_const (pr21 xy)
                     (D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                      pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧))
                  (pr2
                     (# (pair_functor F G)
                        (catbinprodmor (pr11 xy)
                           (pr12 xy)))) @ pr22 xy)) y),,
      idpath
        (pr2
           (# (pair_functor F G)
              (pr1
                 ((λ xy : hfiber # F (pr1 cd2)
                          × hfiber # G (pr2 cd2),
                   catbinprodmor (pr11 xy) (pr12 xy),,
                   total2_paths_f (pr21 xy)
                     (toforallpaths
                        (λ _ : (λ ..., ...) (# F ...),
                         (λ _ : ..., D2 ⟦ ..., ... ⟧)

                        (pr2
                           (# (pair_functor F G)
                              (catbinprodmor ... ...))) @
                      pr22 xy)) y)))) @
      maponpaths pr2
        (let X :=
           pr2
             ((λ xy : hfiber # F (pr1 cd2)
                      × hfiber # G (pr2 cd2),
               catbinprodmor (pr11 xy) (pr12 xy),,
               total2_paths_f (pr21 xy)
                 (toforallpaths

                        ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),

                        ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),

                    (pr2
                       (# (pair_functor F G)
                          (catbinprodmor (pr11 xy)
                             (pr12 xy)))) @ pr22 xy))
                y) in
         X)) = pr11 y
 apply idpath.
          
C1, C2, D1, D2: category
F: C1 ⟶ C2
G: D1 ⟶ D2
F_ff: fully_faithful F
G_ff: fully_faithful G
cd, cd': category_binproduct C1 D1
cd2: category_binproduct C2 D2 ⟦ 
pair_functor F G cd, pair_functor F G cd' ⟧
y: hfiber # F (pr1 cd2) × hfiber # G (pr2 cd2)
transportf
  (λ x : C1 ⟦ pr1 cd, pr1 cd' ⟧, # F x = pr1 cd2)
  (idpath (pr11 y))
  (pr21 ((pr11 ((λ xy : hfiber # F (pr1 cd2)
                        × hfiber # G (pr2 cd2),
                 catbinprodmor (pr11 xy) (pr12 xy),,
                 total2_paths_f (pr21 xy)
                   (toforallpaths
                      (λ _ : (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd),
                                    F (pr1 cd') ⟧,
                              D2
                              ⟦ pr2
                                  (pair_functor F G cd),
                              pr2
                                (pair_functor F G cd')
                              ⟧) (# F (pr11 xy)),

                              F (pr1 cd') ⟧,
                        D2
                        ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                        pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧)
                         (pr1 cd2))
                      (transportf
                         (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd),
                                F (pr1 cd') ⟧,
                          D2
                          ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                          pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧)
                         (pr21 xy))
                      (idfun
                         (D2
                          ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                          pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧))
                      (transportf_const (pr21 xy)

                          ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                          pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧))
                      (pr2

                            (catbinprodmor (pr11 xy)
                               (pr12 xy)))) @ pr22 xy))
                  y),,
          maponpaths pr1
            (pr2
               ((λ xy : hfiber # F (pr1 cd2)
                        × hfiber # G (pr2 cd2),
                 catbinprodmor (pr11 xy) (pr12 xy),,
                 total2_paths_f (pr21 xy)
                   (toforallpaths
                      (λ _ : (λ _ : C2 ⟦ ..., ... ⟧,
                              D2 ⟦ pr2 ..., pr2 ... ⟧)
                               (# F (pr11 xy)),
                       (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F ..., F ... ⟧,
                        D2 ⟦ pr2 (...), pr2 (...) ⟧)
                         (pr1 cd2))
                      (transportf
                         (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (...), F (...)
                                ⟧,
                          D2
                          ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                          pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧)
                         (pr21 xy))
                      (idfun
                         (D2
                          ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                          pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧))
                      (transportf_const (pr21 xy)
                         (D2
                          ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                          pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧))
                      (pr2
                         (# (pair_functor F G)
                            (catbinprodmor (pr11 xy)
                               (pr12 xy)))) @ pr22 xy))
                  y))),,
         pr21 ((λ xy : hfiber # F (pr1 cd2)
                       × hfiber # G (pr2 cd2),
                catbinprodmor (pr11 xy) (pr12 xy),,
                total2_paths_f (pr21 xy)
                  (toforallpaths
                     (λ _ : (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd),
                                   F (pr1 cd') ⟧,
                             D2
                             ⟦ pr2
                                 (pair_functor F G cd),
                             pr2
                               (pair_functor F G cd')

                      (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd),
                             F (pr1 cd') ⟧,
                       D2 ⟦ pr2 (pair_functor F G cd),
                       pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧)
                        (pr1 cd2))
                     (transportf
                        (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd),
                               F (pr1 cd') ⟧,

                         pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧))

                         pr2 (pair_functor F G cd') ⟧))
                     (pr2

                           (catbinprodmor (pr11 xy)
                              (pr12 xy)))) @ pr22 xy))

           (pr2
              (# (pair_functor F G)

                    ((λ xy : hfiber # F (pr1 cd2)
                             × hfiber # G (pr2 cd2),
                      catbinprodmor (pr11 xy)

                       (pr2
                          (# (pair_functor F G)
                             (catbinprodmor ... ...))) @
                     pr22 xy)) y) in
            X))) = pr21 y

C1, C2, D1, D2: category
F: C1 ⟶ C2
G: D1 ⟶ D2
F_ff: fully_faithful F
G_ff: fully_faithful G

F: C1 ⟶ C2
G: D1 ⟶ D2

G_ff: fully_faithful G

     (λ _ : hfiber # F (pr1 cd2), hfiber # G (pr2 cd2))
     (total2_paths_f (idpath (pr11 y))

                             (pr12 y),,

                                (λ _ : D2 ⟦ pr2 (...),

                                    pr2 (...) ⟧))

     (pr2

C1, C2, D1, D2: category
F: C1 ⟶ C2
G: D1 ⟶ D2
F_ff: fully_faithful F
G_ff: fully_faithful G
cd, cd': category_binproduct C1 D1
cd2: category_binproduct C2 D2 ⟦ 
pair_functor F G cd, pair_functor F G cd' ⟧
y: hfiber # F (pr1 cd2) × hfiber # G (pr2 cd2)
transportf

  ?p
  (pr2
     (transportf
        (λ _ : hfiber # F (pr1 cd2),
         hfiber # G (pr2 cd2))
        (total2_paths_f (idpath (pr11 y))
           (let X :=
              λ (C : category)

              (x0 x'0 : x = x'),

            X C2 (F (pr1 cd)) 
              (F (pr1 cd')) 
              (# F (pr11 y))

                        (idfun (...))

                        (pr21 y) 
                        (...)) 
                        (pr2 (...)) @ pr22 y)),,
                        maponpaths pr1

                        ... @ pr22 y)))),,

C1, C2, D1, D2: category
F: C1 ⟶ C2

G_ff: fully_faithful G

pr1
  (transportf
     (λ _ : hfiber # F (pr1 cd2), hfiber # G (pr2 cd2))
     (total2_paths_f (idpath (pr11 y))
        (let X :=
           λ (C : category) (a b : C)
           (x x' : C ⟦ a, b ⟧) (x0 x'0 : x = x'),
           pr1 (C a b x x' x0 x'0) in
         X C2 (F (pr1 cd)) (F (pr1 cd'))
           (# F (pr11 y)) (pr1 cd2)
           (transportf
              (λ x : C1 ⟦ pr1 cd, pr1 cd' ⟧,
               # F x = pr1 cd2) (idpath (pr11 y))
              (pr21 ((pr11 (catbinprodmor (pr11 y)
                              (pr12 y),,
                            total2_paths_f (pr21 y)
                              (toforallpaths
                                 (λ _ : D2 ⟦ pr2 ...,
                                        pr2 ... ⟧,

                               pr22 y)),,
                      maponpaths pr1
                        (pr2
                           (catbinprodmor (pr11 y)

                                    ...) (pr2 ...) @
                               pr22 y)))),,
                     pr21 (catbinprodmor (pr11 y)
                             (pr12 y),,

                                       pr2 (...) ⟧,

                                     (pair_functor F G

                                   (pair_functor F G

                                          ... ⟧,

                                    pr2 (...) ⟧))
                                (pr2
                                   (# (pair_functor F
                                         G)
                                      (catbinprodmor
                                         ... ...))) @
                              pr22 y)),,
                     idpath
                       (pr2
                          (# (pair_functor F G)
                             (pr1
                                (catbinprodmor
                                   (pr11 y) (pr12 y),,
                                 total2_paths_f
                                   (pr21 y) (...))))) @
                     maponpaths pr2
                       (let X0 :=
                          pr2
                            (catbinprodmor (pr11 y)
                               (pr12 y),,
                             total2_paths_f (pr21 y)
                               (toforallpaths ... ...
                                  ... ... ... @ pr22 y))
                          in
                        X0)))) (pr21 y)))
     (pr2
        ((pr11 ((λ xy : hfiber # F (pr1 cd2)
                        × hfiber # G (pr2 cd2),

C1, C2, D1, D2: category
F: C1 ⟶ C2
G: D1 ⟶ D2
F_ff: fully_faithful F
G_ff: fully_faithful G
cd, cd': category_binproduct C1 D1
cd2: category_binproduct C2 D2 ⟦ 
pair_functor F G cd, pair_functor F G cd' ⟧
y: hfiber # F (pr1 cd2) × hfiber # G (pr2 cd2)
pr1
  (transportf
     (λ _ : hfiber # F (pr1 cd2), hfiber # G (pr2 cd2))
     (paths_rect (# F (pr11 y) = pr1 cd2)
        (maponpaths pr1
           (total2_paths_f (pr21 y)
              (toforallpaths
                 (λ _ : D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧,
                  D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧)
                 (transportf
                    (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd),
                           F (pr1 cd') ⟧,
                     D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧)
                    (pr21 y))
                 (idfun
                    (D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧))
                 (transportf_const (pr21 y)
                    (D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧))
                 (# G (pr12 y)) @ pr22 y)))
        (λ (b2 : # F (pr11 y) = pr1 cd2)
         (_ : maponpaths pr1
                (total2_paths_f (pr21 y)
                   (toforallpaths
                      (λ _ : D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd),
                             G (pr2 cd') ⟧,
                       D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧)
                      (transportf
                         (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd),
                                F (pr1 cd') ⟧,
                          D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd')
                          ⟧) (pr21 y))
                      (idfun
                         (D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd')
                          ⟧))
                      (transportf_const (pr21 y)
                         (D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd')
                          ⟧)) (# G (pr12 y)) @ pr22 y)) =
              b2),
         pr11 y,,
         maponpaths pr1
           (total2_paths_f (pr21 y)
              (toforallpaths
                 (λ _ : D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧,
                  D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧)
                 (transportf
                    (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd),
                           F (pr1 cd') ⟧,
                     D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧)
                    (pr21 y))
                 (idfun
                    (D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧))
                 (transportf_const (pr21 y)
                    (D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧))
                 (# G (pr12 y)) @ pr22 y)) =
         pr11 y,, b2)
        (idpath
           (pr11 y,,
            maponpaths pr1
              (total2_paths_f (pr21 y)
                 (toforallpaths
                    (λ _ : D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd),
                           G (pr2 cd') ⟧,
                     D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧)
                    (transportf
                       (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd),
                              F (pr1 cd') ⟧,
                        D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧)
                       (pr21 y))
                    (idfun
                       (D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧))
                    (transportf_const (pr21 y)
                       (D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧))
                    (# G (pr12 y)) @ pr22 y))))
        (pr21 y)
        (pr1
           (C2 (F (pr1 cd)) (F (pr1 cd'))
              (# F (pr11 y)) (pr1 cd2)
              (maponpaths pr1
                 (total2_paths_f (pr21 y)
                    (toforallpaths
                       (λ _ : D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd),
                              G (pr2 cd') ⟧,
                        D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧)
                       (transportf
                          (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd),
                                 F (pr1 cd') ⟧,
                           D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd),
                           G (pr2 cd') ⟧) (pr21 y))
                       (idfun
                          (D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd),
                           G (pr2 cd') ⟧))
                       (transportf_const (pr21 y)
                          (D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd),
                           G (pr2 cd') ⟧))
                       (# G (pr12 y)) @ pr22 y)))
              (pr21 y))))
     (pr12 y,,
      maponpaths pr2
        (total2_paths_f (pr21 y)
           (toforallpaths
              (λ _ : D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧,
               D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧)
              (transportf
                 (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd), F (pr1 cd') ⟧,
                  D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧)
                 (pr21 y))
              (idfun (D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧))
              (transportf_const (pr21 y)
                 (D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧))
              (# G (pr12 y)) @ pr22 y)))) = pr12 y

            
C1, C2, D1, D2: category
F: C1 ⟶ C2
G: D1 ⟶ D2
F_ff: fully_faithful F
G_ff: fully_faithful G

pr1
  (transportf
     (λ _ : hfiber # F (pr1 cd2), hfiber # G (pr2 cd2))
     (paths_rect (# F (pr11 y) = pr1 cd2)
        (maponpaths pr1
           (total2_paths_f (pr21 y)
              (toforallpaths
                 (λ _ : D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧,
                  D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧)
                 (transportf
                    (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd),
                           F (pr1 cd') ⟧,
                     D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧)

                 (transportf_const (pr21 y)
                    (D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧))
                 (# G (pr12 y)) @ pr22 y)))
        (λ (b2 : # F (pr11 y) = pr1 cd2)
         (_ : maponpaths pr1
                (total2_paths_f (pr21 y)
                   (toforallpaths
                      (λ _ : D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd),
                             G (pr2 cd') ⟧,

                                F (pr1 cd') ⟧,

                      (transportf_const (pr21 y)

              b2),
         pr11 y,,
         maponpaths pr1
           (total2_paths_f (pr21 y)

C1, C2, D1, D2: category
F: C1 ⟶ C2
G: D1 ⟶ D2
F_ff: fully_faithful F
G_ff: fully_faithful G
cd, cd': category_binproduct C1 D1
cd2: category_binproduct C2 D2 ⟦ 
pair_functor F G cd, pair_functor F G cd' ⟧
y: hfiber # F (pr1 cd2) × hfiber # G (pr2 cd2)
transportf
  (λ _ : hfiber # F (pr1 cd2), hfiber # G (pr2 cd2))
  (paths_rect (# F (pr11 y) = pr1 cd2)
     (maponpaths pr1
        (total2_paths_f (pr21 y)
           (toforallpaths
              (λ _ : D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧,
               D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧)
              (transportf
                 (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd), F (pr1 cd') ⟧,
                  D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧)
                 (pr21 y))
              (idfun (D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧))
              (transportf_const (pr21 y)
                 (D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧))
              (# G (pr12 y)) @ pr22 y)))
     (λ (b2 : # F (pr11 y) = pr1 cd2)
      (_ : maponpaths pr1
             (total2_paths_f (pr21 y)
                (toforallpaths
                   (λ _ : D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd')
                          ⟧,
                    D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧)
                   (transportf
                      (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd),
                             F (pr1 cd') ⟧,
                       D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧)
                      (pr21 y))
                   (idfun
                      (D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧))
                   (transportf_const (pr21 y)
                      (D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧))
                   (# G (pr12 y)) @ pr22 y)) = b2),
      pr11 y,,
      maponpaths pr1
        (total2_paths_f (pr21 y)
           (toforallpaths
              (λ _ : D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧,
               D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧)
              (transportf
                 (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd), F (pr1 cd') ⟧,
                  D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧)
                 (pr21 y))
              (idfun (D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧))
              (transportf_const (pr21 y)
                 (D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧))
              (# G (pr12 y)) @ pr22 y)) = pr11 y,, b2)
     (idpath
        (pr11 y,,
         maponpaths pr1
           (total2_paths_f (pr21 y)
              (toforallpaths
                 (λ _ : D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧,
                  D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧)
                 (transportf
                    (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd),
                           F (pr1 cd') ⟧,
                     D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧)
                    (pr21 y))
                 (idfun
                    (D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧))
                 (transportf_const (pr21 y)
                    (D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧))
                 (# G (pr12 y)) @ pr22 y)))) (pr21 y)
     (pr1
        (C2 (F (pr1 cd)) (F (pr1 cd')) (# F (pr11 y))
           (pr1 cd2)
           (maponpaths pr1
              (total2_paths_f (pr21 y)
                 (toforallpaths
                    (λ _ : D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd),
                           G (pr2 cd') ⟧,
                     D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧)
                    (transportf
                       (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd),
                              F (pr1 cd') ⟧,
                        D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧)
                       (pr21 y))
                    (idfun
                       (D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧))
                    (transportf_const (pr21 y)
                       (D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧))
                    (# G (pr12 y)) @ pr22 y)))
           (pr21 y))))
  (pr12 y,,
   maponpaths pr2
     (total2_paths_f (pr21 y)
        (toforallpaths
           (λ _ : D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧,
            D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧)
           (transportf
              (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (pr1 cd), F (pr1 cd') ⟧,
               D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧)
              (pr21 y))
           (idfun (D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧))
           (transportf_const (pr21 y)
              (D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧))
           (# G (pr12 y)) @ pr22 y))) = ?t2

              (D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧))

C1, C2, D1, D2: category
F: C1 ⟶ C2
G: D1 ⟶ D2
F_ff: fully_faithful F
G_ff: fully_faithful G
cd, cd': category_binproduct C1 D1
cd2: category_binproduct C2 D2 ⟦ 
pair_functor F G cd, pair_functor F G cd' ⟧
y: hfiber # F (pr1 cd2) × hfiber # G (pr2 cd2)
transportf
  (λ x : D1 ⟦ pr2 cd, pr2 cd' ⟧, # G x = pr2 cd2)
  (maponpaths pr1
     (internal_paths_rew_r
        (hfiber # G (pr2 cd2) → hfiber # G (pr2 cd2))
        (transportf
           (λ _ : hfiber # F (pr1 cd2),
            hfiber # G (pr2 cd2))
           (paths_rect (# F (pr11 y) = pr1 cd2)
              (maponpaths pr1
                 (total2_paths_f (pr21 y)
                    (toforallpaths
                       (λ _ : D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd),
                              G (pr2 cd') ⟧,
                        D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧)
                       (transportf
                          (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (...), F (...)
                                 ⟧,
                           D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd),
                           G (pr2 cd') ⟧) (pr21 y))
                       (idfun
                          (D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd),
                           G (pr2 cd') ⟧))
                       (transportf_const (pr21 y)
                          (D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd),
                           G (pr2 cd') ⟧))
                       (# G (pr12 y)) @ pr22 y)))
              (λ (b2 : # F (pr11 y) = pr1 cd2)
               (_ : maponpaths pr1
                      (total2_paths_f (pr21 y)
                         (toforallpaths
                            (λ _ : D2 ⟦ G ..., G ... ⟧,
                             D2 ⟦ G (...), G (...) ⟧)
                            (transportf
                               (λ _ : ...,
                                D2 ⟦ ..., ... ⟧)
                               (pr21 y))
                            (idfun
                               (D2 ⟦ G ..., G ... ⟧))
                            (transportf_const (pr21 y)
                               (D2 ⟦ G ..., G ... ⟧))
                            (# G (pr12 y)) @ pr22 y)) =
                    b2),
               pr11 y,,
               maponpaths pr1
                 (total2_paths_f (pr21 y)
                    (toforallpaths
                       (λ _ : D2 ⟦ G ..., G ... ⟧,
                        D2 ⟦ G (...), G (...) ⟧)
                       (transportf
                          (λ _ : ..., D2 ⟦ ..., ... ⟧)
                          (pr21 y))
                       (idfun (D2 ⟦ G ..., G ... ⟧))
                       (transportf_const (pr21 y)
                          (D2 ⟦ G ..., G ... ⟧))
                       (# G (pr12 y)) @ pr22 y)) =
               pr11 y,, b2)
              (idpath
                 (pr11 y,,
                  maponpaths pr1
                    (total2_paths_f (pr21 y)
                       (toforallpaths
                          (λ _ : D2 ⟦ G ..., G ... ⟧,
                           D2 ⟦ G (...), G (...) ⟧)
                          (transportf
                             (λ _ : ...,
                              D2 ⟦ ..., ... ⟧)
                             (pr21 y))
                          (idfun (D2 ⟦ G ..., G ... ⟧))
                          (transportf_const (pr21 y)
                             (D2 ⟦ G ..., G ... ⟧))
                          (# G (pr12 y)) @ pr22 y))))
              (pr21 y)
              (pr1
                 (C2 (F (pr1 cd)) (F (pr1 cd'))
                    (# F (pr11 y)) (pr1 cd2)
                    (maponpaths pr1
                       (total2_paths_f (pr21 y)
                          (toforallpaths
                             (λ _ : D2 ⟦ ..., ... ⟧,
                              D2 ⟦ G ..., G ... ⟧)
                             (transportf (λ ..., ...)
                                (pr21 y))
                             (idfun (D2 ⟦ ..., ... ⟧))
                             (transportf_const
                                (pr21 y)
                                (D2 ⟦ ..., ... ⟧))
                             (# G (pr12 y)) @ pr22 y)))
                    (pr21 y)))))
        (idfun (hfiber # G (pr2 cd2)))
        (λ h : hfiber # G (pr2 cd2)
               → hfiber # G (pr2 cd2),
         h
           (pr12 y,,
            maponpaths pr2
              (total2_paths_f (pr21 y)
                 (toforallpaths
                    (λ _ : D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd),
                           G (pr2 cd') ⟧,
                     D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧)
                    (transportf
                       (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F ..., F ... ⟧,
                        D2 ⟦ G (...), G (...) ⟧)
                       (pr21 y))
                    (idfun
                       (D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧))
                    (transportf_const (pr21 y)
                       (D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧))
                    (# G (pr12 y)) @ pr22 y))) =
         idfun (hfiber # G (pr2 cd2))
           (pr12 y,,
            maponpaths pr2
              (total2_paths_f (pr21 y)
                 (toforallpaths
                    (λ _ : D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd),
                           G (pr2 cd') ⟧,
                     D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧)
                    (transportf
                       (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F ..., F ... ⟧,
                        D2 ⟦ G (...), G (...) ⟧)
                       (pr21 y))
                    (idfun
                       (D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧))
                    (transportf_const (pr21 y)
                       (D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧))
                    (# G (pr12 y)) @ pr22 y))))
        (idpath
           (idfun (hfiber # G (pr2 cd2))
              (pr12 y,,
               maponpaths pr2
                 (total2_paths_f (pr21 y)
                    (toforallpaths
                       (λ _ : D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd),
                              G (pr2 cd') ⟧,
                        D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧)
                       (transportf
                          (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F ..., F ... ⟧,
                           D2 ⟦ G (...), G (...) ⟧)
                          (pr21 y))
                       (idfun
                          (D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd),
                           G (pr2 cd') ⟧))
                       (transportf_const (pr21 y)
                          (D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd),
                           G (pr2 cd') ⟧))
                       (# G (pr12 y)) @ pr22 y)))))
        (transportf_const
           (paths_rect (# F (pr11 y) = pr1 cd2)
              (maponpaths pr1
                 (total2_paths_f (pr21 y)
                    (toforallpaths
                       (λ _ : D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd),
                              G (pr2 cd') ⟧,
                        D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd), G (pr2 cd') ⟧)
                       (transportf
                          (λ _ : C2 ⟦ F (...), F (...)
                                 ⟧,
                           D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd),
                           G (pr2 cd') ⟧) (pr21 y))
                       (idfun
                          (D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd),
                           G (pr2 cd') ⟧))
                       (transportf_const (pr21 y)
                          (D2 ⟦ G (pr2 cd),
                           G (pr2 cd') ⟧))
                       (# G (pr12 y)) @ pr22 y)))
              (λ (b2 : # F (pr11 y) = pr1 cd2)
               (_ : maponpaths pr1
                      (total2_paths_f (pr21 y)
                         (toforallpaths
                            (λ _ : D2 ⟦ G ..., G ... ⟧,
                             D2 ⟦ G (...), G (...) ⟧)
                            (transportf
                               (λ _ : ...,
                                D2 ⟦ ..., ... ⟧)
                               (pr21 y))
                            (idfun
                               (D2 ⟦ G ..., G ... ⟧))
                            (transportf_const (pr21 y)
                               (D2 ⟦ G ..., G ... ⟧))
                            (# G (pr12 y)) @ pr22 y)) =
                    b2),
               pr11 y,,
               maponpaths pr1
                 (total2_paths_f (pr21 y)
                    (toforallpaths
                       (λ _ : D2 ⟦ G ..., G ... ⟧,
                        D2 ⟦ G (...), G (...) ⟧)
                       (transportf
                          (λ _ : ..., D2 ⟦ ..., ... ⟧)
                          (pr21 y))
                       (idfun (D2 ⟦ G ..., G ... ⟧))
                       (transportf_const (pr21 y)
                          (D2 ⟦ G ..., G ... ⟧))
                       (# G (pr12 y)) @ pr22 y)) =
               pr11 y,, b2)
              (idpath
                 (pr11 y,,
                  maponpaths pr1
                    (total2_paths_f (pr21 y)
                       (toforallpaths
                          (λ _ : D2 ⟦ G ..., G ... ⟧,
                           D2 ⟦ G (...), G (...) ⟧)
                          (transportf
                             (λ _ : ...,
                              D2 ⟦ ..., ... ⟧)
                             (pr21 y))
                          (idfun (D2 ⟦ G ..., G ... ⟧))
                          (transportf_const (pr21 y)
                             (D2 ⟦ G ..., G ... ⟧))
                          (# G (pr12 y)) @ pr22 y))))
              (pr21 y)
              (pr1
                 (C2 (F (pr1 cd)) (F (pr1 cd'))
                    (# F (pr11 y)) (pr1 cd2)
                    (maponpaths pr1
                       (total2_paths_f (pr21 y)
                          (toforallpaths
                             (λ _ : D2 ⟦ ..., ... ⟧,
                              D2 ⟦ G ..., G ... ⟧)
                             (transportf (λ ..., ...)
                                (pr21 y))
                             (idfun (D2 ⟦ ..., ... ⟧))
                             (transportf_const
                                (pr21 y)
                                (D2 ⟦ ..., ... ⟧))
                             (# G (pr12 y)) @ pr22 y)))
                    (pr21 y)))) (hfiber # G (pr2 cd2)))) @
   idpath (pr12 y)
   :
   pr1
     (transportf
        (λ _ : hfiber # F (pr1 cd2),
         hfiber # G (pr2 cd2))
        (total2_paths_f (idpath (pr11 y))
           (let X :=
              λ (C : category) (a b : C)
              (x x' : C ⟦ a, b ⟧) (x0 x'0 : x = x'),
              pr1 (C a b x x' x0 x'0) in
            X C2 (F (pr1 cd)) (F (pr1 cd'))
              (# F (pr11 y)) (pr1 cd2)
              (transportf
                 (λ x : C1 ⟦ pr1 cd, pr1 cd' ⟧,
                  # F x = pr1 cd2) (idpath (pr11 y))
                 (pr21 ((pr11 (catbinprodmor (pr11 y)
                                 (pr12 y),,
                               total2_paths_f (pr21 y)
                                 (toforallpaths (...)
                                    (...) (...) (...)
                                    (...) @ pr22 y)),,
                         maponpaths pr1
                           (pr2
                              (catbinprodmor (pr11 y)
                                 (pr12 y),,
                               total2_paths_f (pr21 y)
                                 (...)))),,
                        pr21 (catbinprodmor (pr11 y)
                                (pr12 y),,
                              total2_paths_f (pr21 y)
                                (toforallpaths
                                   (λ ..., ...)

                                      ... ...)
                                   (pr2 ...) @ pr22 y)),,

                             (# (pair_functor F G)
                                (pr1 ...))) @
                        maponpaths pr2
                          (let X0 := pr2 (...,, ...)
                             in
                           X0)))) (pr21 y)))
        (pr2
           ((pr11 ((λ xy : hfiber # F (pr1 cd2)
                           × hfiber # G (pr2 cd2),
                    catbinprodmor (pr11 xy) (pr12 xy),,
                    total2_paths_f (pr21 xy)
                      (toforallpaths
                         (λ _ : ... ..., (...) (...))
                         (transportf (λ ..., ...)
                            (pr21 xy))
                         (idfun (D2 ⟦ ..., ... ⟧))
                         (transportf_const (pr21 xy)
                            (D2 ⟦ ..., ... ⟧))
                         (pr2 (# ... ...)) @ pr22 xy))
                     y),,
             maponpaths pr1
               (pr2
                  ((λ xy : hfiber # F (pr1 cd2)
                           × hfiber # G (pr2 cd2),
                    catbinprodmor (pr11 xy) (pr12 xy),,
                    total2_paths_f (pr21 xy)
                      (toforallpaths (...) (...) (...)
                         (...) (...) @ pr22 xy)) y))),,
            pr21 ((λ xy : hfiber # F (pr1 cd2)
                          × hfiber # G (pr2 cd2),
                   catbinprodmor (pr11 xy) (pr12 xy),,
                   total2_paths_f (pr21 xy)
                     (toforallpaths
                        (λ _ : (...) (...),
                         (λ ..., ...) (pr1 cd2))
                        (transportf
                           (λ _ : ..., D2 ⟦ ..., ... ⟧)
                           (pr21 xy))

                      pr22 xy)) y),,
            idpath
              (pr2
                 (# (pair_functor F G)
                    (pr1
                       ((λ xy : ... × ...,
                         catbinprodmor ... ...,,
                         total2_paths_f ... ...) y)))) @
            maponpaths pr2
              (let X :=
                 pr2

                            × hfiber # G (...),
                     catbinprodmor (pr11 xy) (pr12 xy),,

               X)))) = pr12 y)
  (pr2
     (transportf
        (λ _ : hfiber # F (pr1 cd2),

                 (# (pair_functor F G)
                    (pr1
                       ((λ xy : hfiber # F (...)
                                × hfiber # G (...),

            maponpaths pr2
              (let X :=
                 pr2
                   ((λ xy : hfiber # F (pr1 cd2)
                            × hfiber # G (pr2 cd2),

                     total2_paths_f (pr21 xy)
                       (toforallpaths (...) (...)
                          (...) (...) (...) @ pr22 xy))
                      y) in
               X))))) = pr22 y
 apply homset_property.
    
C1, C2, D1, D2: category
F: C1 ⟶ C2
G: D1 ⟶ D2
F_ff: fully_faithful F
G_ff: fully_faithful G
cd, cd': category_binproduct C1 D1
cd2: category_binproduct C2 D2 ⟦ 
pair_functor F G cd, pair_functor F G cd' ⟧
hfiberprod: hfiber # (pair_functor F G) cd2
≃ hfiber # F (pr1 cd2)
  × hfiber # G (pr2 cd2)
iscontr (hfiber # (pair_functor F G) cd2)

C1, C2, D1, D2: category

C1, C2, D1, D2: category
F: C1 ⟶ C2
G: D1 ⟶ D2
F_ff: fully_faithful F
G_ff: fully_faithful G
cd, cd': category_binproduct C1 D1
cd2: category_binproduct C2 D2 ⟦ 
pair_functor F G cd, pair_functor F G cd' ⟧
hfiberprod: hfiber # (pair_functor F G) cd2
≃ hfiber # F (pr1 cd2)
  × hfiber # G (pr2 cd2)
iscontr (hfiber # F (pr1 cd2))
 apply (F_ff (pr1 cd) (pr1 cd') (pr1 cd2)).
    
C1, C2, D1, D2: category
F: C1 ⟶ C2
G: D1 ⟶ D2
F_ff: fully_faithful F
G_ff: fully_faithful G
cd, cd': category_binproduct C1 D1
cd2: category_binproduct C2 D2 ⟦ 
pair_functor F G cd, pair_functor F G cd' ⟧
hfiberprod: hfiber # (pair_functor F G) cd2
≃ hfiber # F (pr1 cd2)
  × hfiber # G (pr2 cd2)
iscontr (hfiber # G (pr2 cd2))
 apply (G_ff (pr2 cd) (pr2 cd') (pr2 cd2)).
  Qed.

d2: ∑ a : D1, z_iso (G a) (pr2 cd2)

C1, C2, D1, D2: category
F: C1 ⟶ C2
G: D1 ⟶ D2
F_eso: essentially_surjective F
G_eso: essentially_surjective G
cd2: category_binproduct C2 D2
d1: ∑ a : C1, z_iso (F a) (pr1 cd2)
d2: ∑ a : D1, z_iso (G a) (pr2 cd2)
z_iso (F (pr1 (pr1 d1,, pr1 d2))) (pr1 cd2)
C1, C2, D1, D2: category
F: C1 ⟶ C2
G: D1 ⟶ D2
F_eso: essentially_surjective F
G_eso: essentially_surjective G
cd2: category_binproduct C2 D2
d1: ∑ a : C1, z_iso (F a) (pr1 cd2)
d2: ∑ a : D1, z_iso (G a) (pr2 cd2)
z_iso (G (pr2 (pr1 d1,, pr1 d2))) (pr2 cd2)

    
C1, C2, D1, D2: category
F: C1 ⟶ C2
G: D1 ⟶ D2
F_eso: essentially_surjective F
G_eso: essentially_surjective G
cd2: category_binproduct C2 D2
d1: ∑ a : C1, z_iso (F a) (pr1 cd2)
d2: ∑ a : D1, z_iso (G a) (pr2 cd2)
z_iso (F (pr1 (pr1 d1,, pr1 d2))) (pr1 cd2)
 exact (pr2 d1).
    
C1, C2, D1, D2: category
F: C1 ⟶ C2
G: D1 ⟶ D2
F_eso: essentially_surjective F
G_eso: essentially_surjective G
cd2: category_binproduct C2 D2
d1: ∑ a : C1, z_iso (F a) (pr1 cd2)
d2: ∑ a : D1, z_iso (G a) (pr2 cd2)
z_iso (G (pr2 (pr1 d1,, pr1 d2))) (pr2 cd2)
 exact (pr2 d2).
  Qed.

End WeakEquivalenceProperties.

End LiftedFunctorsComposition.

Section LiftedFunctorsPairFunctor.

  
C1, C2, D1, D2, E1, E2: category
F1: C1 ⟶ D1
F2: D1 ⟶ E1
G1: C2 ⟶ D2
G2: D2 ⟶ E2
nat_z_iso (pair_functor (F1 ∙ F2) (G1 ∙ G2))
  (pair_functor F1 G1 ∙ pair_functor F2 G2)

  
C1, C2, D1, D2, E1, E2: category
F1: C1 ⟶ D1
F2: D1 ⟶ E1
G1: C2 ⟶ D2
G2: D2 ⟶ E2
nat_z_iso (pair_functor (F1 ∙ F2) (G1 ∙ G2))
  (pair_functor F1 G1 ∙ pair_functor F2 G2)

F1: C1 ⟶ D1

  (pair_functor F1 G1 ∙ pair_functor F2 G2)
  ((λ x : category_binproduct C1 C2,
    catbinprodmor
      (identity (F2 (pr1 (pair_functor F1 G1 x))))
      (identity (G2 (pr2 (pair_functor F1 G1 x)))))
   :
   nat_trans_data (pair_functor (F1 ∙ F2) (G1 ∙ G2))
     (pair_functor F1 G1 ∙ pair_functor F2 G2))

          [ exact (id_right _ @ ! id_left _) | rewrite transportf_const ; exact (id_right _ @ ! id_left _) ]).

        (pair_functor F1 G1 ∙ pair_functor F2 G2))

        G1 G2))

     (let X := λ c : C1, pr1 (pr2 α c) in X (pr1 c))
     (let X := λ c : C2, pr1 (pr2 β c) in X (pr2 c)))
 abstract (split ; (use total2_paths_f ; [apply (pr2 α) | rewrite transportf_const ; apply (pr2 β)])).
  Defined.

  Context {C1 C2 C1' C2' D1 D2 : category}
          (D1' D2' : univalent_category)
          {F1 : functor C1 D1}
          {F2 : functor C2 D2}
          (F1' : functor C1' D1')
          (F2' : functor C2' D2')
          (F1_eso : essentially_surjective F1)
          (F2_eso : essentially_surjective F2)
          (F1_ff : fully_faithful F1)
          (F2_ff : fully_faithful F2).

  Let FF := pair_functor F1 F2.
  Let FF' := pair_functor F1' F2'.

  Let FF_eso := pair_functor_eso _ _ F1_eso F2_eso.
  Let FF_ff := pair_functor_ff _ _ F1_ff F2_ff.

  Let DD' := (_ ,, is_univalent_category_binproduct (pr2 D1') (pr2 D2')) : univalent_category.

  
C1, C2, C1', C2', D1, D2: category
D1', D2': univalent_category
F1: C1 ⟶ D1
F2: C2 ⟶ D2
F1': C1' ⟶ D1'
F2': C2' ⟶ D2'
F1_eso: essentially_surjective F1
F2_eso: essentially_surjective F2
F1_ff: fully_faithful F1
F2_ff: fully_faithful F2
FF:= pair_functor F1 F2: category_binproduct C1 C2
⟶ category_binproduct D1 D2
FF':= pair_functor F1' F2': category_binproduct C1' C2'
⟶ category_binproduct D1' D2'
FF_eso:= pair_functor_eso F1 F2 F1_eso F2_eso: essentially_surjective (pair_functor F1 F2)
FF_ff:= pair_functor_ff F1 F2 F1_ff F2_ff: fully_faithful (pair_functor F1 F2)
DD':= category_binproduct (pr1 D1') (pr1 D2'),,
is_univalent_category_binproduct 
  (pr2 D1') (pr2 D2'): univalent_category
H1: C1 ⟶ C1'
H2: C2 ⟶ C2'
nat_z_iso
  (lift_functor_along DD' FF FF_eso FF_ff
     (pair_functor H1 H2 ∙ pair_functor F1' F2'))
  (pair_functor
     (lift_functor_along D1' F1 F1_eso F1_ff
        (H1 ∙ F1'))
     (lift_functor_along D2' F2 F2_eso F2_ff
        (H2 ∙ F2')))

F2: C2 ⟶ D2

F2': C2' ⟶ D2'

Section LiftedFunctorsProperties.

  
C, D, E: category
F1, F2: C ⟶ D
α: nat_z_iso F1 F2
G: D ⟶ E
nat_z_iso (F1 ∙ G) (F2 ∙ G)

  
C, D, E: category
F1, F2: C ⟶ D
α: nat_z_iso F1 F2
G: D ⟶ E
nat_z_iso (F1 ∙ G) (F2 ∙ G)

    
C, D, E: category
F1, F2: C ⟶ D
α: nat_z_iso F1 F2
G: D ⟶ E
F1 ∙ G ⟹ F2 ∙ G
C, D, E: category
F1, F2: C ⟶ D
α: nat_z_iso F1 F2
G: D ⟶ E
is_nat_z_iso ?μ

    
C, D, E: category
F1, F2: C ⟶ D
α: nat_z_iso F1 F2
G: D ⟶ E
is_nat_z_iso ?μ

  Defined.

  Context {C : category} (D : univalent_category)
            (F1 : functor C D)

  Let FFF_ff := pair_functor_ff _ _ FF_ff F1_ff.
  Let FFF_eso := pair_functor_eso _ _ FF_eso F1_eso.

  Let FFF' := pair_functor F1 FF.
  Let FFF'_ff := pair_functor_ff _ _ F1_ff FF_ff.
  Let FFF'_eso := pair_functor_eso _ _ F1_eso FF_eso.

  Let DDD' := (_ ,, is_univalent_category_binproduct (pr2 D) (pr2 DD)) : univalent_category.
